function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

if (!is_file('dev/vendor_update.sh')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: dev/vendor_update.sh');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('dev/vendor_update.sh')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): dev/vendor_update.sh');
	} else if (sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') != '745ae549698662f35f381ceb5e41eabb8642ba46') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('dev/vendor_update.sh', 0755)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of dev/vendor_update.sh');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '745ae549698662f35f381ceb5e41eabb8642ba46') {
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== 'ac13df0821b2f1b5981025b19618b3c6571b0e9b') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$tmp = pathinfo('dev/vendor_update.sh');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('dev/vendor_update.sh')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('dev/vendor_update.sh', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('dev/vendor_update.sh') !== '745ae549698662f35f381ceb5e41eabb8642ba46') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): dev/vendor_update.sh');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php') != 'b38cb1a082cdb26092a677de2fecbea97f6227b2') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php') !== 'b38cb1a082cdb26092a677de2fecbea97f6227b2') {
		if (@sha1_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php') !== '49c119bddee13d2c4cecb18b97d90690080278c8') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php') !== 'b38cb1a082cdb26092a677de2fecbea97f6227b2') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): includes/simplexml_supplement.inc.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('oidplus.min.css.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.min.css.php');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.css.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') != '4fbea19ce1170f39187fedb6810d133d8234e668') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.css.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.css.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '4fbea19ce1170f39187fedb6810d133d8234e668') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '52cfe19c9fd7288e283f08fbdc29f04f23297d8e') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.css.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.css.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.css.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.css.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.css.php') !== '4fbea19ce1170f39187fedb6810d133d8234e668') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.css.php');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('vendor/cacert.pem')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: vendor/cacert.pem');
	writefile_4();
	if (!is_file('vendor/cacert.pem')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): vendor/cacert.pem');
	} else if (sha1_file('vendor/cacert.pem') != 'f55a08214760a3622a31474d7b02c435334a0290') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): vendor/cacert.pem');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('vendor/cacert.pem', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of vendor/cacert.pem');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('vendor/cacert.pem') !== 'f55a08214760a3622a31474d7b02c435334a0290') {
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/cacert.pem') !== 'f5eb339bc66e442cc3e88cdad2957db3306aa7ff') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: vendor/cacert.pem');
			$tmp = pathinfo('vendor/cacert.pem');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('vendor/cacert.pem')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('vendor/cacert.pem', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('vendor/cacert.pem') !== 'f55a08214760a3622a31474d7b02c435334a0290') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): vendor/cacert.pem');
		}
	}
